            <script>
                var myDate = new Date();
                var daysBefore = 0;
                var dateStr = getDateStr(myDate);
                var addFlag = "today";
                var host_url = '//www.zhibo8.cc';
                $(function(){
                    loadListHtml(dateStr);

                    $(".prev").click(function() {
                        addFlag = "asc";
                        daysBefore++;
                        dateStr = getDateBeforeStr(daysBefore);
                        loadListHtml(dateStr);
                    });
                    $(".next").click(function() {
                        addFlag = "dec";
                        daysBefore--;
                        dateStr = getDateBeforeStr(daysBefore);
                        loadListHtml(dateStr);
                    });
                });

                function loadListHtml(dateStr){
                    var vedioList={};
                    var bifenList={};
                    $.ajax({
                        type: "get",//使用get方法访问后台
                        dataType: "json",//返回json格式的数据
                        url: "//s.qiumibao.com/json/record/"+dateStr+".htm",//要访问的后台地址
                        data: "key=" + Math.random(),//要发送的数据
                        async:false,
                        complete :function(){},//AJAX请求完成
                        success: function(data){
                            vedioList=data['list'];
                        }
                    });
                    $.ajax({
                        type: "get",//使用get方法访问后台
                        dataType: "json",//返回json格式的数据
                        url: "//bifen.qiumibao.com/json/"+dateStr+"/list.htm",//要访问的后台地址
                        data: "key=" + Math.random(),//要发送的数据
                        async:false,
                        complete :function(){},//AJAX请求完成
                        success: function(data){
                            bifenList=array_column(data['list'],'id');
                        }
                    });
                    var htmlStr = "";
                    $.each(vedioList,function(key,v){
                        var k=v['saishi_id'];

                        var show_top10_video = false;
                        if(v['title'].indexOf('十佳球') > -1 || v['title'].indexOf('五佳球') > -1){
                            show_top10_video = true;
                        }
                        console.log('show_top10_video:'+show_top10_video);
                        if(k==0 && !show_top10_video){
                            return true;
                        }

                        if(bifenList[k]!=undefined&&v['type']=='basketball'){
                            var jijinlink = '';
                            if(v['jijin_url']!=''){
                                jijinlink = '<a class="fr m_r_5" href="//www.zhibo8.cc'+v['jijin_url']+'" title="'+v['jijin_title']+'" target="_blank" >集锦</a>';
                            }
                            var luxianglink = '';
                            var left_score=v['left_team']['identity']+'_score',right_score=v['right_team']['identity']+'_score';
                            var real_title=v['left_team']['name']+' '+bifenList[k][left_score]+'-'+bifenList[k][right_score]+' '+v['right_team']['name'];
                            if(bifenList[k]['period_cn']=='完赛'&&bifenList[k]['home_score']!=''&&bifenList[k]['home_score']>0&&bifenList[k]['visit_score']!=''&&bifenList[k]['visit_score']>0){
                                //real_title=v['left_team']['name']+' '+bifenList[k][left_score]+'-'+bifenList[k][right_score]+' '+v['right_team']['name'];
                            }else{
                                real_title=v['left_team']['name']+' vs '+v['right_team']['name'];
                            }
                            if(v['luxiang_url']!=''){
                                luxianglink= '<a class="fr m_r_5" href="//www.zhibo8.cc'+v['luxiang_url']+'" title="'+v['luxiang_title']+'" target="_blank" >录像</a>';
                            }
                            htmlStr += "<li>"+real_title + " " + luxianglink + " " + jijinlink +  "</li>\n";
                        }else if(show_top10_video&&v['type']=='basketball'){
                            var jijinlink = '';
                            if(v['jijin_url']!=''){
                                jijinlink = '<a class="fr m_r_5" href="//www.zhibo8.cc'+v['jijin_url']+'" title="'+v['jijin_title']+'" target="_blank" >集锦</a>';
                            }
                            var luxianglink = '';
                            if(v['luxiang_url']!=''){
                                luxianglink= '<a class="fr m_r_5" href="//www.zhibo8.cc'+v['luxiang_url']+'" title="'+v['luxiang_title']+'" target="_blank" >录像</a>';
                            }
                            real_title = v['title'].substr(0, v['title'].indexOf("-"));
                            if(jijinlink || luxianglink){
                                htmlStr += "<li>"+ real_title + " " + luxianglink + " " + jijinlink +  "</li>\n";
                            }
                        }
                    });
                    if(htmlStr == ""){
                        $("#video_date_list ul").html("<li>当日无比赛视频</li>");
                    }else{
                        $("#video_date_list ul").html(htmlStr);
                    }
                    $(".curTime").html(turnDateStr(dateStr));
                }

                function getDateStr(myDate){
                    var year = myDate.getFullYear();
                    var month = myDate.getMonth() + 1;
                    if(month<10)month = "0"+month;
                    var date  = myDate.getDate();
                    if(date<10)date = "0"+date;
                    var dateStr = year+"-"+month+"-"+date;
                    return dateStr;
                }
                function getDateBeforeStr(n){
                    var date = new Date();
                    date.setDate(date.getDate()-n);
                    return getDateStr(date);
                }
                function turnDateStr(dateStr){
                    var tmpArr = dateStr.split("-");
                    return tmpArr[1]+"月"+tmpArr[2]+"日";
                }
                function array_column(arr,key){
                    var res={};
                    $.each(arr,function(k,v){
                        if(v[key]>0){
                            res[v[key]]=v;
                        }
                    });
                    return res;
                }
